\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb14e}{14e}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb27c}{27c}, \verb@prev_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb27c}{27c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Accumulating Definitions}

There are three steps required to handle a definition:
\begin{enumerate}
  \item Build an entry for the name so we can look it up later.
  \item Collect the scrap and save it in the table of scraps.
  \item Attach the scrap to the name.
\end{enumerate}
We go through the same steps for both file names and fragment names.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap44}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb27e}{} $\langle\,${\it Build output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {27e}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_file_name(); /* returns a pointer to the name entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int scrap = collect_scrap();      /* returns an index to the scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb28b}{28b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb26}{26}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_file_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb124}{124}, \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb96b}{96b}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap45}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb28a}{} $\langle\,${\it Build fragment definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {28a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_macro_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int scrap = collect_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb28b}{28b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb26}{26}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_macro_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb126}{126}, \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb96b}{96b}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Since a file or fragment may be defined by many scraps, we maintain them
in a simple linked list. The list is actually built in reverse order,
with each new definition being added to the head of the list.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap46}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb28b}{} $\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {28b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *def = (Scrap_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Scrap_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  def->scrap = scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  def->quoted = quoted;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  def->next = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  name->defs = def;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb27e}{27e}\NWlink{nuweb28a}{, 28a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap47}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb28c}{} $\langle\,${\it Skip over an in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {28c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while ((c = source_get()) != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over at-sign or go to skipped}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb29a}{29a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected EOF in text at (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@skipped:  ;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb26}{26}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap48}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb29a}{} $\langle\,${\it Skip over at-sign or go to skipped}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {29a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '}': case ']': case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        goto skipped;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case 'x': case '|': case ',': case '<':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '>': case '%': case '1': case '2':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '3': case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '7': case '8': case '9': case '_':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case 'f': case '#': case '+': case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case 'v': case '*': case 'c': case '\'':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (c != nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected %c%c in text at (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb28c}{28c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Block Comments}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap49}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb29b}{} $\langle\,${\it Collect a block comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {29b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char * p = blockBuff;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char * e = blockBuff + (sizeof(blockBuff)/sizeof(blockBuff[0])) - 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip whitespace}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb30a}{30a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while (p < e)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add one char to the block buffer}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb30b}{30b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (p == e)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip to the next nw-char}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb32b}{32b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   *p = '\000';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb26}{26}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@blockBuff@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb32c}{32c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap50}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb30a}{} $\langle\,${\it Skip whitespace}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {30a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@while (source_peek == ' '@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       || source_peek == '\t'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       || source_peek == '\n')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   (void)source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb29b}{29b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap51}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb30b}{} $\langle\,${\it Add one char to the block buffer}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {30b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add an at character to the block or break}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb31a}{31a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else if (c == EOF)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   source_ungetc(&c);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add any other character to the block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb31b}{31b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb29b}{29b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_ungetc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb88}{88}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap52}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb31a}{} $\langle\,${\it Add an at character to the block or break}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {31a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int cc = source_peek;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (cc == 'c')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while (c <= ' ');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else if (cc == 'd'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == 'D'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == 'q'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == 'Q'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == 'o'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == 'O'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         || cc == EOF)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   source_ungetc(&c);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   *p++ = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb30b}{30b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_ungetc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb88}{88}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap53}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb31b}{} $\langle\,${\it Add any other character to the block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {31b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps skip white-space}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb32a}{32a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb30b}{30b}.

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap54}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb32a}{} $\langle\,${\it Perhaps skip white-space}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {32a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (c == ' ')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while (source_peek == ' ')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (c == '\n')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (source_peek == '\n')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (source_peek == '\n');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb31b}{31b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap55}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb32b}{} $\langle\,${\it Skip to the next nw-char}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {32b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@while ((c = source_get()), c != nw_char && c != EOF)/* Skip */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@source_ungetc(&c);@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{flushleft}
We don't show block comments inside scraps in the \TeX\ file,
but we do show where they go.

\begin{flushleft} \small

\item{}

\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
The block comment is presently in the block buffer. Here we
copy it into the scrap whence we shall copy it into the output
file.

\begin{flushleft} \small

\mbox{}\verb@   do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      push(c, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = *p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while (c != '\0');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@   int bgn = indent + global_indent;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int posn = bgn + strlen(comment_begin[comment_flag]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps put a delayed indent}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb112b}{112b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(comment_begin[comment_flag], file);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Move a word to the file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb33c}{33c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it If we break the line at this word}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb34a}{34a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc('\n', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         for (i = 0; i < bgn ; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c != '\0')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            posn = bgn + strlen(comment_mid[comment_flag]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            fputs(comment_mid[comment_flag], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(comment_end[comment_flag], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\subsection{Fixing the Cross References}

Since the definition and reference lists for each name are accumulated
in reverse order, we take the time at the end of \verb|pass1| to
reverse them all so they'll be simpler to print out prettily.
The code for \verb|reverse_lists| appears in Section~\ref{names}.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap64}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb34d}{} $\langle\,${\it Reverse cross-reference lists}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {34d}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(file_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(macro_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(user_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb25b}{25b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@file_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117b}{117b}, \verb@macro_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117b}{117b}, \verb@reverse_lists@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb133c}{133c}, \verb@user_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117b}{117b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Dealing with fragment parameters}

Fragment parameters were added on later in nuweb's development.
There still is not, for example, an index of fragment parameters.
We need a data type to keep track of fragment parameters.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap65}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb34e}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {34e}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@typedef int *Parameters;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14b}{14b}\NWlink{nuweb34e}{, 34e}\NWlink{nuweb92b}{, 92b}\NWlink{nuweb92c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb93a}{, 93a}\NWlink{nuweb93c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb94a}{, 94a}\NWlink{nuweb94b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb95c}{, 95c}\NWlink{nuweb95d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb96a}{, 96a}\NWlink{nuweb96b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb102a}{, 102a}\NWlink{nuweb102c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb103a}{, 103a}\NWlink{nuweb103b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb104a}{, 104a}\NWlink{nuweb105a}{, 105a}\NWlink{nuweb106a}{, 106a}\NWlink{nuweb115a}{, 115a}\NWlink{nuweb134b}{, 134b}\NWlink{nuweb134c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135a}{, 135a}\NWlink{nuweb135b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb135c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb136a}{, 136a}\NWlink{nuweb136b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb136c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb138a}{, 138a}\NWlink{nuweb139b}{, 139b}\NWlink{nuweb139c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb144a}{, 144a}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb145a}{, 145a}\NWlink{nuweb146b}{, 146b}\NWlink{nuweb147b}{, 147b}\NWlink{nuweb148a}{, 148a}\NWlink{nuweb148c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@Parameters@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb37}{37}\NWlink{nuweb105a}{, 105a}\NWlink{nuweb106a}{, 106a}\NWlink{nuweb107}{, 107}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
When we are copying a scrap to the output, we check for an embedded
parameter. If we find it we copy it. Otherwise it's an old-style
parameter and we can then pull
the $n$th string from the \verb|Parameters| list when we
see an \verb|@1| \verb|@2|, etc.

\begin{flushleft} \small\label{scrap66}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb35}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle macro parameter substitution}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {35}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Arglist * args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Name * name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        lookup(c - '1', inArgs, inParams, &name, &args);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (name == (Name *)1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Embed_Node * q = (Embed_Node *)args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          indent = write_scraps(file, spelling, q->defs,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                global_indent + indent,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                indent_chars, debug_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                tab_flag, indent_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                0,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                q->args, inParams,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                local_parameters, "");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        else if (name != NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           int i, narg;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           Arglist *q = args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps comment this macro}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb112a}{112a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          indent = write_scraps(file, spelling, name->defs,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                global_indent + indent,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                indent_chars, debug_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                tab_flag, indent_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                comment_flag, args, name->arg,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                local_parameters, p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        else if (args != NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           if (delayed_indent) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Put out the indent}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108d}{108d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           fputs((char *)args, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        else if ( parameters && parameters[c - '1'] ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Scrap_Node param_defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          param_defs.scrap = parameters[c - '1'];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          param_defs.next = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          write_scraps(file, spelling, &param_defs,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       global_indent + indent,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       indent_chars, debug_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       tab_flag, indent_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       comment_flag, NULL, NULL, 0, "");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        } else if (delayed_indent) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Put out the indent}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108d}{108d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb109c}{109c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Arglist@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb129b}{129b}, \verb@delayed_indent@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106b}{106b}, \verb@Embed_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb132d}{132d}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb103b}{103b}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}, \verb@write_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106a}{106a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Now onto actually parsing fragment parameters from a call.
We start off checking for fragment parameters, an \verb|@(| sequence
followed by parameters separated by \verb|@,| sequences, and
terminated by a \verb|@)| sequence.

We collect separate scraps for each parameter, and write the
scrap numbers down in the text. For example, if the file has:
\begin{verbatim}
   @<foo @( param1 @, param2 @)@>
\end{verbatim}
we actually make new scraps, say 10 and 11, for param1 and param2,
and write in the collected scrap:
\begin{verbatim}
   @<foo @(10@,11@)@>
\end{verbatim}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap67}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb36}{} $\langle\,${\it Save macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {36}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int param_scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char param_buf[10];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  push('(', &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     param_scrap = collect_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sprintf(param_buf, "%d", param_scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     pushs(param_buf, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     push(scrap_ended_with, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     add_to_use(name, current_scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while( scrap_ended_with == ',' );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while( ' ' == c );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != '>') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    /* ZZZ print error */;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb101c}{101c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@add_to_use@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb102a}{102a}, \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb96b}{96b}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@push@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb95d}{95d}, \verb@pushs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb96a}{96a}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
If we get inside, we have at least one parameter, which will be at
the beginning of the parms buffer, and we prime the pump with the
first character.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap68}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb37}{} $\langle\,${\it Check for macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {37}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '(') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Parameters res = arena_getmem(10 * sizeof(int));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int *p2 = res;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int count = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int scrapnum;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while( c && c != ')' ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      scrapnum = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while( '0' <= c && c <= '9' ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        scrapnum = scrapnum  * 10 + c - '0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if ( c == nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p2++ = scrapnum;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (count < 10) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p2++ = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      count++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while( c && c != nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if ( c == nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *parameters = res;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb105b}{105b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@Parameters@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb34e}{34e}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb102c}{102c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
These are used in \verb|write_tex| and \verb|write_html| to output the
argument list for a fragment.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap69}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb38}{} $\langle\,${\it Format macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {38}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char sep;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   sep = '(';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(sep,file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs("{\\footnotesize ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     write_single_scrap_ref(file, scraps + 1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fprintf(file, "\\label{scrap%d}\n", scraps + 1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs(" }", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_last = '{';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     copy_scrap(file, TRUE, NULL);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     ++scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sep = ',';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while ( source_last != ')' && source_last != EOF );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(" ) ",file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while(c != nw_char && c != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb59}{59}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb54}{54}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94b}{94b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap70}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb39a}{} $\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {39a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char sep;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\

\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(sep,file);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_last = '{';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     copy_scrap(file, TRUE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     ++scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sep = ',';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while ( source_last != ')' && source_last != EOF );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(" ) ",file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while(c != nw_char && c != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\end{rawhtml}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\item{}

\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\section{Writing the Latex File} \label{latex-file}

The second pass (invoked via a call to \verb|write_tex|) copies most of
the text from the source file straight into a \verb|.tex| file.
Definitions are formatted slightly and cross-reference information is
printed out.

Note that all the formatting is handled in this section.
If you don't like the format of definitions or indices or whatever,
it'll be in this section somewhere. Similarly, if someone wanted to
modify nuweb to work with a different typesetting system, this would
be the place to look.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap71}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb39b}{} $\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {39b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void write_tex();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb25a}{25a}\NWlink{nuweb39b}{, 39b}\NWlink{nuweb52b}{, 52b}\NWlink{nuweb55b}{, 55b}\NWlink{nuweb69a}{, 69a}\NWlink{nuweb82b}{, 82b}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb93b}{, 93b}\NWlink{nuweb102b}{, 102b}\NWlink{nuweb114b}{, 114b}\NWlink{nuweb118a}{, 118a}\NWlink{nuweb128d}{, 128d}\NWlink{nuweb139a}{, 139a}\NWlink{nuweb148d}{, 148d}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb10}{10}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@write_tex@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40b}{40b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We need a few local function declarations before we get into the body
of \verb|write_tex|.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap72}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb40a}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {40a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap();             /* formats the body of a scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers();      /* formats a list of scrap numbers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_entry();             /* formats an index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_file_entry();        /* formats a file index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void write_arg();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void write_literal();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void write_ArglistElement();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb54}{54}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}, \verb@format_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb64b}{64b}\NWlink{nuweb79c}{, 79c}, \verb@format_file_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb62b}{62b}, \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb67c}{67c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb50b}{50b}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{, 75c}, \verb@write_arg@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb45b}{45b}, \verb@write_ArglistElement@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb61}{61}, \verb@write_literal@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb53}{53}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
The routine \verb|write_tex| takes two file names as parameters: the
name of the web source file and the name of the \verb|.tex| output file.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap73}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb40b}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {40b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void write_tex(file_name, tex_name, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *file_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *tex_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *tex_file = fopen(tex_name, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (tex_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "writing %s\n", tex_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_open(file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb41a}{41a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|tex_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb41c}{41c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open %s\n", command_name, tex_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_tex@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb24b}{24b}\NWlink{nuweb39b}{, 39b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb92a}{92a}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Now that the \verb|\NW...| macros are used, it seems convenient
to write default definitions for those macros so that source files
need not define anything new. If a user wants to change any of
the macros (to use hyperref or to write in some language other than
english) he or she can redefine the commands.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap74}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb41a}{} $\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {41a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (hyperref_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtarget}[2]{\\hypertarget{#1}{#2}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWlink}[2]{\\hyperlink{#1}{#2}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtarget}[2]{#2}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWlink}[2]{#2}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroDefBy}{Fragment defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroRefIn}{Fragment referenced in}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroNoRef}{Fragment never referenced}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtDefBy}{Defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtRefIn}{Referenced in}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtNoRef}{Not referenced}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtFileDefBy}{File defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsUsed}{Uses:}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsNotUsed}{Never used}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsDefed}{Defines:}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWsep}{${\\diamond}$}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWnotglobal}{(not defined globally)}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWuseHyperlinks}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (hyperoptions[0] != '\0')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write the hyperlink usage macro}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb41b}{41b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb40b}{40b}\NWlink{nuweb70a}{, 70a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@hyperoptions@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@hyperref_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@Uses@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb144c}{144c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap75}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb41b}{} $\langle\,${\it Write the hyperlink usage macro}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {41b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@fprintf(tex_file, "\\usepackage[%s]{hyperref}", hyperoptions);@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb41a}{41a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@hyperoptions@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We make our second (and final) pass through the source web, this time
copying characters straight into the \verb|.tex| file. However, we keep
an eye peeled for \verb|@|~characters, which signal a command sequence.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap76}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb41c}{} $\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|tex_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {41c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int inBlock = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Interpret at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb42a}{42a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(c, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb40b}{40b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap77}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb42a}{} $\langle\,${\it Interpret at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {42a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int big_definition = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          nw_char = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          update_delimit_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'Q':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'D': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'q':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'd': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb44b}{44b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 's':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Step to next sector}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb27a}{27a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'S':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Close the current sector}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb27b}{27b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb48c}{48c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy label from source into}\nobreak\ ({\footnotesize 42b\label{scrap78}
 }\mbox{}\verb@tex_file@ ) {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57b}{57b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'c': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin or end a block comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb34c}{34c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb62a}{62a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'm': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of macro names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb63b}{63b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'u': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb67b}{67b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'v': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy version info into tex file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb43}{43}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            putc(c, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb41c}{41c}.

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap79}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb43}{} $\langle\,${\it Copy version info into tex file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {43}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@fputs(version_string, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb42a}{42a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@version_string@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Formatting Definitions}

We go through a fair amount of effort to format a file definition.
I've derived most of the \LaTeX\ commands experimentally; it's quite
likely that an expert could do a better job. The \LaTeX\ for
the previous fragment definition should look like this (perhaps modulo
the scrap references):
{\small
\begin{verbatim}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap70}\raggedright\small
$\langle$Interpret at-sequence {\footnotesize 18}$\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int big_definition = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @$\langle$Write output file definition {\footnotesize 19a}$\rangle$\verb@@\\
\end{verbatim}
\vdots
\begin{verbatim}
\mbox{}\verb@    case '@{\tt @}\verb@': putc(c, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@$\diamond$
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item Fragment referenced in scrap 17b.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\end{verbatim}}

\noindent
The {\em flushleft\/} environment is used to avoid \LaTeX\ warnings
about underful lines. The {\em minipage\/} environment is used to
avoid page breaks in the middle of scraps. The {\em verb\/} command
allows arbitrary characters to be printed (however, note the special
handling of the \verb|@| case in the switch statement).

Fragment and file definitions are formatted nearly identically.
I've factored the common parts out into separate scraps.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap80}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb44a}{} $\langle\,${\it Write output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {44a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_file_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46a}{46a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWtarget{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{} ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(tex_file, "\\verb%c\"%s\"%c\\nobreak\\ {\\footnotesize {", nw_char, name->spelling, nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}}$\\equiv$\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb47}{47}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb48d}{48d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if ( scrap_flag ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write file defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb49b}{49b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_defs_refs(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_uses_refs(tex_file, scraps++);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb49a}{49a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb48a}{48a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb42a}{42a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_file_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb124}{124}, \verb@format_defs_refs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb146b}{146b}, \verb@format_uses_refs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb145a}{145a}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@scrap_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94b}{94b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
I don't format a fragment name at all specially, figuring the programmer
might want to use italics or bold face in the midst of the name.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap81}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb44b}{} $\langle\,${\it Write macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {44b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_macro_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46a}{46a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWtarget{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{} $\\langle\\,${\\it ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write the macro's name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb45a}{45a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}\\nobreak\\ {\\footnotesize {", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}}$\\,\\rangle\\equiv$\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb47}{47}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb48d}{48d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb49c}{49c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro refs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb50a}{50a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_defs_refs(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_uses_refs(tex_file, scraps++);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb49a}{49a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb48a}{48a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap82}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb45a}{} $\langle\,${\it Write the macro's name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {45a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int i = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (*p != '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (*p == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_arg(tex_file, name->arg[i++]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputc(*p++, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44b}{44b}\NWlink{nuweb65b}{, 65b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@ARG_CHR@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb127c}{127c}, \verb@write_arg@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb45b}{45b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap83}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb45b}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {45b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void write_arg(FILE * tex_file, char * p)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\hbox{\\slshape\\sffamily ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while (*p)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      switch (*p)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '$':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '_':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '^':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '#':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         fputc('\\', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputc(*p, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\/}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_arg@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb45a}{, 45a}\NWlink{nuweb56a}{, 56a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap84}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb46a}{} $\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {46a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (big_definition)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (inBlock)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it End block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46d}{46d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\begin{flushleft} \\small", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (inBlock)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Switch block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46c}{46c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Start block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46b}{46b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(tex_file, "\\label{scrap%d}\\raggedright\\small\n", scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}\NWlink{nuweb44b}{b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap85}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb46b}{} $\langle\,${\it Start block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {46b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\begin{flushleft} \\small\n\\begin{minipage}{\\linewidth}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@inBlock = TRUE;@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb34c}{34c}\NWlink{nuweb46a}{, 46a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.

\end{list}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap86}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb46c}{} $\langle\,${\it Switch block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {46c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\par\\vspace{\\baselineskip}\n",  tex_file);@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb46a}{46a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.

\end{list}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap87}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb46d}{} $\langle\,${\it End block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {46d}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\end{minipage}\\vspace{4ex}\n",  tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\end{flushleft}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@inBlock = FALSE;@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb34c}{34c}\NWlink{nuweb46a}{, 46a}\NWlink{nuweb48a}{, 48a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
The interesting things here are the $\diamond$ inserted at the end of
each scrap and the various spacing commands. The diamond helps to
clearly indicate the end of a scrap. The spacing commands were derived
empirically; they may be adjusted to taste.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap88}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb47}{} $\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {47}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\vspace{-1ex}\n\\begin{list}{}{} \\item\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  extra_scraps = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  copy_scrap(tex_file, TRUE, name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("{\\NWsep}\n\\end{list}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}\NWlink{nuweb44b}{b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb54}{54}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\newpage
\noindent
We've got one last spacing command, controlling the amount of white
space after a scrap.

Note also the whitespace eater. I use it to remove any blank lines
that appear after a scrap in the source file. This way, text following
a scrap will not be indented. Again, this is a matter of personal taste.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap89}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb48a}{} $\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {48a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  scraps += extra_scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (big_definition)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\vspace{4ex}\n\\end{flushleft}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it End block}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb46d}{46d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}\NWlink{nuweb44b}{b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap90}\raggedright\small

\vspace{-1ex}

\end{list}

\end{flushleft}
\subsubsection{Formatting Cross References}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap92}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb48d}{} $\langle\,${\it Begin the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {48d}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\vspace{-1.5ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\footnotesize\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}\NWlink{nuweb44b}{b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
There may (unusually) be nothing to output in the cross-reference
section, so output an empty list item anyway to avoid having an empty
list.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap93}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb49a}{} $\langle\,${\it Finish the cross-reference environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {49a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\n\\item{}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\n\\end{list}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb44a}{44a}\NWlink{nuweb44b}{b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap94}\raggedright\small

\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->defs->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\item \\NWtxtFileDefBy\\ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, name->defs);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            "would have crashed in 'Write file defs' for '%s'\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap97}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb50b}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {50b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, scraps)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *tex_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Scrap_Node *scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  scraps = scraps->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (scraps) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    scraps = scraps->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(".\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb49b}{, 49b}\NWlink{nuweb49c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb50a}{, 50a}\NWlink{nuweb63a}{, 63a}\NWlink{nuweb66b}{, 66b}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb74a}{, 74a}\NWlink{nuweb74b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb74c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{, 75c}\NWlink{nuweb80b}{, 80b}\NWlink{nuweb80d}{d}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94a}{94a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsubsection{Formatting a Scrap}

We add a \verb|\mbox{}| at the beginning of each line to avoid
problems with older versions of \TeX.
This is the only place we really care whether a scrap is
delimited with \verb|@{...@}|, \verb|@[...@]|, or \verb|@(...@)|,
and we base our output sequences on that.

We have an array \texttt{delimit\_scrap} where we store our strings
that perform the formatting for one line of a scrap. Upon
initialisation we copy our strings from the source
\texttt{orig\_delimit\_scrap} to it to have the strings writeable.  We
might change the strings later when we encounter the command to change
the `nuweb character'.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap98}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb51}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {51}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static char *orig_delimit_scrap[3][5] = {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {} mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "\\verb@{\tt @}\verb@", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "@{\tt @}\verb@{\\tt @{\tt @}\verb@}\\verb@{\tt @}\verb@", "\\mbox{}", "\\\\" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* [] mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "", "", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "", "" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* () mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "$", "$", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "", "" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@};@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static char *delimit_scrap[3][5];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
The function \texttt{initialise\_delimit\_scrap\_array} does the
copying. If we want to have the listings package \index{listings package}
do the formatting we have to replace only two of those strings: the
\texttt{verb} command has to be replaced by the package's \texttt{lstinline}
command.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap99}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb52a}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {52a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void initialise_delimit_scrap_array() {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int i,j;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for(i = 0; i < 3; i++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for(j = 0; j < 5; j++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if((delimit_scrap[i][j] = strdup(orig_delimit_scrap[i][j])) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* replace verb by lstinline */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    free(delimit_scrap[0][0]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if((delimit_scrap[0][0]=strdup("\\lstinline@{\tt @}\verb@")) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    free(delimit_scrap[0][2]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if((delimit_scrap[0][2]=strdup("@{\tt @}\verb@{\\tt @{\tt @}\verb@}\\lstinline@{\tt @}\verb@")) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap100}\raggedright\small

\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void initialise_delimit_scrap_array(void);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap101}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb52c}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {52c}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int scrap_type = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.

\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap102}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb53}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {53}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void write_literal(FILE * tex_file, char * p, int mode)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fprintf(tex_file, "", p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(delimit_scrap[mode][0], tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while (*p!= '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     if (*p == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputs(delimit_scrap[mode][2], tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputc(*p, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(delimit_scrap[mode][1], tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_literal@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb59}{, 59}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap103}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb54}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {54}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap(file, prefix, name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int prefix;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name * name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char ** params = name->arg;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '{') scrap_type = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '[') scrap_type = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '(') scrap_type = 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][3], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][4], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 fputs("\n", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][3], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb55c}{55c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb56a}{56a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb38}{38}\NWlink{nuweb39a}{, 39a}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb47}{, 47}\NWlink{nuweb48c}{, 48c}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb73c}{, 73c}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}, \verb@scrap_type@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb32d}{32d}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{, 52c}\NWlink{nuweb56a}{, 56a}\NWlink{nuweb58a}{, 58a}\NWlink{nuweb58b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb59}{, 59}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
When we encounter the command to change the `nuweb character' we call
this function. It updates the scrap formatting directives accordingly.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap104}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb55a}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {55a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void update_delimit_scrap()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static int been_here_before = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode begin */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][0][10] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][0][5] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode end */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][1][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][2][6] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][2][18] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][2][13] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* []-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[1][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* ()-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[2][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}

\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
