\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy label from source into}\nobreak\ ({\footnotesize 56b\label{scrap108}
 }\mbox{}\verb@file@ ) {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57b}{57b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'v': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy version info into file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57a}{57a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '*':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57d}{57d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}': fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              return;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb59}{59}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '%': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip commented-out code}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57e}{57e}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Bold Keyword}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb58a}{58a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 't': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Italic "\verb@fragment title@"}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb58b}{58b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Italic "\verb@file name@"}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb58b}{58b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              if (name == NULL@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                  || name->arg[c - '1'] == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][2], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                fputc(c,   file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                write_arg(file, name->arg[c - '1']);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][2], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          /* ignore these since pass1 will have warned about them */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

\NWtarget{nuweb59}{} $\langle\,${\it Format macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {59}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *args = collect_scrap_name(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = args->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *q = args->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int narg = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1],file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\hbox{", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("$\\langle\\,${\\it ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (*p != '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (*p == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (q == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         write_literal(file, name->arg[narg], scrap_type);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_ArglistElement(file, q, params);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        q = q->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      narg++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputc(*p++, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}\\nobreak\\ ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (scrap_name_has_parameters) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb38}{38}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(file, "{\\footnotesize ");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write abbreviated definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb60}{60}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}$\\,\\rangle$", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs("}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap118}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb61}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {61}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void@\\
\mbox{}\verb@write_ArglistElement(FILE * file, Arglist * args, char ** params)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = args->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *q = args->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char * p = (char*)q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (p[0] == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       write_arg(file, params[p[1] - '1']);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       write_literal(file, (char *)q, 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else if (name == (Name *)1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node * qq = (Scrap_Node *)q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    qq->quoted = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scraps(file, "", qq,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 -1, "", 0, 0, 0, 0,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 NULL, params, 0, "");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    extra_scraps++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    qq->quoted = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("$\\langle\\,${\\it ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (*p != '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (*p == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_ArglistElement(file, q, params);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        q = q->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         fputc(*p++, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}\\nobreak\\ ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (scrap_name_has_parameters) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb38}{38}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(file, "{\\footnotesize ");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->defs)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write abbreviated definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb60}{60}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "%s: never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}$\\,\\rangle$", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12e}{12e}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb40b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb45b}{, 45b}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{, 50b}\NWlink{nuweb51}{, 51}\NWlink{nuweb52a}{, 52a}\NWlink{nuweb52c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb53}{, 53}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb55a}{, 55a}\NWlink{nuweb61}{, 61}\NWlink{nuweb62b}{, 62b}\NWlink{nuweb64a}{, 64a}\NWlink{nuweb64b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb67a}{, 67a}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}.

\vspace{-1ex}

\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int i = j - 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   Name * kj = @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily key\/}\verb@[j];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Name * ki = @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily key\/}\verb@[i];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (@\hbox{\slshape\sffamily ordering\/}\verb@)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily key\/}\verb@[i + 1] = ki;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      i -= 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while (i >= 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily key\/}\verb@[i + 1] = kj;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('?', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb65b}{65b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94a}{94a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap130}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb66b}{} $\langle\,${\it Write referencing scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {66b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *p = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("{\\footnotesize ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("{\\NWtxtRefIn}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (p->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      /* fputs("s ", tex_file); */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc('.', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("{\\NWtxtNoRef}.", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  putc('}', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap131}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb67a}{} \verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {67a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int has_sector(name, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Name * name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while(name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->sector == sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (has_sector(name->llink, sector))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   return FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@has_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb63b}{63b}\NWlink{nuweb67b}{, 67b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap132}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb67b}{} $\langle\,${\it Write index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {67b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == '+') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (has_sector(user_names, sector)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\n{\\small\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      format_user_entry(user_names, tex_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\end{list}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

\begin{flushleft} \small

\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *tex_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_user_entry(name->llink, tex_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format a user index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb68}{68}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb67b}{, 67b}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb81a}{, 81a}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}.
\item{}
\end{list}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small\label{scrap134}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb68}{} $\langle\,${\it Format a user index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {68}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (name->sector == sector){@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *uses = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if ( uses || dangling_flag ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *defs = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(tex_file, "\\item \\verb%c%s%c: ", nw_char,name->spelling,nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!uses) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("(\\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("})}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (!defs || uses->scrap < defs->scrap) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (uses || defs) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (uses && (!defs || uses->scrap < defs->scrap)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (uses && defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs(", \\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        putc('}', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(".\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb67c}{67c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@dangling_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94a}{94a}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94b}{94b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\section{Writing the LaTeX File with HTML Scraps} \label{html-file}

The HTML generated is patterned closely upon the {\LaTeX} generated in
the previous section.\footnote{\relax While writing this section, I
tried to follow Preston's style as displayed in
Section~\ref{latex-file}---J. D. R.}  When a file name ends in
\verb|.hw|, the second pass (invoked via a call to \verb|write_html|)
copies most of the text from the source file straight into a
\verb|.tex| file.  Definitions are formatted slightly and
cross-reference information is printed out.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap135}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb69a}{} $\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {69a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void write_html();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb25a}{25a}\NWlink{nuweb39b}{, 39b}\NWlink{nuweb52b}{, 52b}\NWlink{nuweb55b}{, 55b}\NWlink{nuweb69a}{, 69a}\NWlink{nuweb82b}{, 82b}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb93b}{, 93b}\NWlink{nuweb102b}{, 102b}\NWlink{nuweb114b}{, 114b}\NWlink{nuweb118a}{, 118a}\NWlink{nuweb128d}{, 128d}\NWlink{nuweb139a}{, 139a}\NWlink{nuweb148d}{, 148d}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb10}{10}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@write_html@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb70a}{70a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We need a few local function declarations before we get into the body
of \verb|write_html|.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap136}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb69b}{} \verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {69b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap();               /* formats the body of a scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void display_scrap_ref();        /* formats a scrap reference */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void display_scrap_numbers();    /* formats a list of scrap numbers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers();      /* pluralizes scrap formats list */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_entry();             /* formats an index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_file_entry();        /* formats a file index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb13a}{13a}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb70a}{, 70a}\NWlink{nuweb75a}{, 75a}\NWlink{nuweb75b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}\NWlink{nuweb79c}{, 79c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb54}{54}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}, \verb@display_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb75b}{75b}, \verb@display_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb75a}{75a}, \verb@format_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb64b}{64b}\NWlink{nuweb79c}{, 79c}, \verb@format_file_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb62b}{62b}, \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb67c}{67c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb50b}{50b}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{, 75c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
The routine \verb|write_html| takes two file names as parameters: the
name of the web source file and the name of the \verb|.tex| output file.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap137}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb70a}{} \verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {70a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void write_html(file_name, html_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *file_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *html_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *html_file = fopen(html_name, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *tex_file = html_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb41a}{41a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (html_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "writing %s\n", html_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_open(file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|html_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb70b}{70b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open %s\n", command_name, html_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb13a}{13a}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb70a}{, 70a}\NWlink{nuweb75a}{, 75a}\NWlink{nuweb75b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}\NWlink{nuweb79c}{, 79c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_html@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb24b}{24b}\NWlink{nuweb69a}{, 69a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb92a}{92a}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We make our second (and final) pass through the source web, this time
copying characters straight into the \verb|.tex| file. However, we keep
an eye peeled for \verb|@|~characters, which signal a command sequence.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap138}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb70b}{} $\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|html_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {70b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Interpret HTML at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb71}{71}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(c, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb70a}{70a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap139}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb71}{} $\langle\,${\it Interpret HTML at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {71}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          nw_char = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          update_delimit_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb72a}{72a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'Q':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'q':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'D':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'd': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb72c}{72c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb78c}{78c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'm': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of macro names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb79a}{79a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'u': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb81a}{81a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            putc(c, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb70b}{70b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@update_delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb55a}{55a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Formatting Definitions}

We go through only a little amount of effort to format a definition.
The HTML for the previous fragment definition should look like this
(perhaps modulo the scrap references):

\begin{verbatim}
<pre>
<a name="nuweb68">&lt;Interpret HTML at-sequence 68&gt;</a> =
{
  c = source_get();
  switch (c) {
    case 'O':
    case 'o': &lt;Write HTML output file definition <a href="#nuweb69">69</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'D':
    case 'd': &lt;Write HTML macro definition <a href="#nuweb71">71</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'f': &lt;Write HTML index of file names <a href="#nuweb86">86</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'm': &lt;Write HTML index of macro names <a href="#nuweb87">87</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'u': &lt;Write HTML index of user-specified names <a href="#nuweb93">93</a>&gt;
              break;
    default:
         if (c==nw_char)
           putc(c, html_file);
         c = source_get();
              break;
  }
}&lt;&gt;</pre>
Fragment referenced in scrap <a href="#nuweb67">67</a>.
<br>
\end{verbatim}

Fragment and file definitions are formatted nearly identically.
I've factored the common parts out into separate scraps.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap140}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb72a}{} $\langle\,${\it Write HTML output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {72a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_file_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin HTML scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb73b}{73b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML output file declaration}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb72b}{72b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  scraps++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of HTML scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb73c}{73c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML file defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb74a}{74a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish HTML scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb73d}{73d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap141}\raggedright\small

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
I don't format a fragment name at all specially, figuring the programmer
might want to use italics or bold face in the midst of the name.  Note
that in this implementation, programmers may only use directives in
fragment names that are recognized in preformatted text elements (PRE).

Modification 2001--02--15.: I'm interpreting the fragment name
as regular LaTex, so that any formatting can be used in it. To use
HTML formatting, the \verb|rawhtml| environment should be used.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap143}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb73a}{} $\langle\,${\it Write HTML macro declaration}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {73a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("<a name=\"nuweb", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(html_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\">&lt;\\end{rawhtml}", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(name->spelling, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{rawhtml} ", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(html_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("&gt;</a> =\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb72c}{72c}.

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}

end the paragraph.

\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb49b}{, 49b}\NWlink{nuweb49c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb50a}{, 50a}\NWlink{nuweb50b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb63a}{, 63a}\NWlink{nuweb66b}{, 66b}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb74a}{, 74a}\NWlink{nuweb74b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb74c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb80b}{, 80b}\NWlink{nuweb80d}{d}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@display_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb75b}{75b}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsubsection{Formatting a Scrap}

We must translate HTML special keywords into entities in scraps.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap153}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb76}{} \verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {76}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap(file, prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '<' : fputs("&lt;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '>' : fputs("&gt;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '&' : fputs("&amp;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': fputc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb55c}{55c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check HTML at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb77}{77}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb13a}{13a}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb70a}{, 70a}\NWlink{nuweb75a}{, 75a}\NWlink{nuweb75b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb75c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}\NWlink{nuweb79c}{, 79c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb38}{38}\NWlink{nuweb39a}{, 39a}\NWlink{nuweb40a}{, 40a}\NWlink{nuweb47}{, 47}\NWlink{nuweb48c}{, 48c}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb73c}{, 73c}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap154}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb77}{} $\langle\,${\it Check HTML at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {77}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '*':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57d}{57d}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')': return;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML bold tag or end}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb79b}{79b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(nw_char, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(c,   file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb78a}{78a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '%': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip commented-out code}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57e}{57e}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             fputc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          /* ignore these since pass1 will have warned about them */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb76}{76}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@pass1@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb25b}{25b}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
There's no need to check for errors here, since we will have already
pointed out any during the first pass.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap155}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb78a}{} $\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {78a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist * args = collect_scrap_name(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = args->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("&lt;\\end{rawhtml}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(name->spelling, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (scrap_name_has_parameters) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb39a}{39a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{rawhtml} ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML abbreviated definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb78b}{78b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("&gt;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb77}{77}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Arglist@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb129b}{129b}, \verb@collect_scrap_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb130}{130}, \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap156}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb78b}{} $\langle\,${\it Write HTML abbreviated definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {78b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item

\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *p = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  display_scrap_ref(file, p->scrap);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(", ... ", file);@\\

\subsection{Generating the Indices}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap157}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb78c}{} $\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {78c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (file_names) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\begin{rawhtml}\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("<dl compact>\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_entry(file_names, html_file, TRUE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("</dl>\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\end{rawhtml}\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb71}{71}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb67c}{67c}\NWlink{nuweb81b}{, 81b}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@user_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117b}{117b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap166}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb81b}{} \verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {81b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry(name, html_file, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *html_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_user_entry(name->llink, html_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format a user HTML index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb82a}{82a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb40a}{40a}\NWlink{nuweb67b}{, 67b}\NWlink{nuweb67c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb69b}{, 69b}\NWlink{nuweb81a}{, 81a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap167}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb82a}{} $\langle\,${\it Format a user HTML index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {82a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *uses = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (uses) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *defs = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(html_file, "<dt><code>%s</code>:\n<dd> ", name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (uses->scrap < defs->scrap) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      display_scrap_ref(html_file, uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("<strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      display_scrap_ref(html_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("</strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (uses || defs) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(", ", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (uses && (!defs || uses->scrap < defs->scrap)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        display_scrap_ref(html_file, uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (uses && defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("<strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        display_scrap_ref(html_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("</strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(".\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb81b}{81b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@display_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb75a}{75a}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}

\end{flushleft}
\verb|MAX_INDENT| defines the maximum number of leading whitespace
 characters. This is only a problem when outputting very long lines,
 possibly by multiple definitions of the same fragment (as in a list
 of elements which is added to every time a new element is defined).

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap170}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb83b}{} $\langle\,${\it Type declarations}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {83b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#define MAX_INDENT 500@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}\NWlink{nuweb83b}{, 83b}\NWlink{nuweb116d}{, 116d}\NWlink{nuweb117a}{, 117a}\NWlink{nuweb127c}{, 127c}\NWlink{nuweb129b}{, 129b}\NWlink{nuweb132d}{, 132d}\NWlink{nuweb144c}{, 144c}\NWlink{nuweb150c}{, 150c}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb10}{10}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@MAX_INDENT@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb83c}{83c}\NWlink{nuweb108a}{, 108a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap171}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb83c}{} $\langle\,${\it Write out \verb|files->spelling|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {83c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static char temp_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static char real_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static int temp_name_count = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char indent_chars[MAX_INDENT];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int temp_file_fd;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *temp_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Find a free temporary file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb84a}{84a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  sprintf(real_name, "%s%s%s", dirpath, path_sep, files->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "writing %s [%s]\n", files->spelling, temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scraps(temp_file, files->spelling, files->defs, 0, indent_chars,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               files->debug_flag, files->tab_flag, files->indent_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               files->comment_flag, NULL, NULL, 0, files->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Move the temporary file to the target, if required}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb84b}{84b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb83a}{83a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@MAX_INDENT@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb83b}{83b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@write_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106a}{106a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap172}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb84a}{} $\langle\,${\it Find a free temporary file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {84a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@for( temp_name_count = 0; temp_name_count < 10000; temp_name_count++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  sprintf(temp_name,"%s%snw%06d", dirpath, path_sep, temp_name_count);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#ifdef O_EXCL@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (-1 != (temp_file_fd = open(temp_name, O_CREAT|O_WRONLY|O_EXCL))) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     temp_file = fdopen(temp_file_fd, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (0 != (temp_file = fopen(temp_name, "a"))) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     if ( 0L == ftell(temp_file)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        temp_file = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#endif@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (!temp_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't create %s for a temporary file\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb83c}{83c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Note the call to \verb|remove| before \verb|rename| -- the ANSI/ISO C
standard does {\em not} guarantee that renaming a file to an existing
filename will overwrite the file.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap173}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb84b}{} $\langle\,${\it Move the temporary file to the target, if required}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {84b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (compare_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Compare the temp file and the old file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb85a}{85a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  remove(real_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Rename the temporary file to the target}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb85b}{85b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb83c}{83c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@compare_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@remove@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Again, we use a call to \verb|remove| before \verb|rename|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap174}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb85a}{} $\langle\,${\it Compare the temp file and the old file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {85a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *old_file = fopen(real_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (old_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int x, y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    temp_file = fopen(temp_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      x = getc(old_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      y = getc(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    } while (x == y && x != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(old_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (x == y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(real_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Rename the temporary file to the target}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb85b}{85b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Rename the temporary file to the target}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb85b}{85b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb84b}{84b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@remove@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap175}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb85b}{} $\langle\,${\it Rename the temporary file to the target}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {85b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (0 != rename(temp_name, real_name)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't rename output file to %s\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, real_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\chapter{The Support Routines}

\section{Source Files} \label{source-files}

\subsection{Global Declarations}

We need two routines to handle reading the source files.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap176}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb86a}{} $\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {86a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void source_open(); /* pass in the name of the source file */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@extern int source_get();   /* no args; returns the next char or EOF */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@extern int source_last;   /* what last source_get() returned. */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@extern int source_peek;   /* The next character to get */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb25a}{25a}\NWlink{nuweb39b}{, 39b}\NWlink{nuweb52b}{, 52b}\NWlink{nuweb55b}{, 55b}\NWlink{nuweb69a}{, 69a}\NWlink{nuweb82b}{, 82b}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb93b}{, 93b}\NWlink{nuweb102b}{, 102b}\NWlink{nuweb114b}{, 114b}\NWlink{nuweb118a}{, 118a}\NWlink{nuweb128d}{, 128d}\NWlink{nuweb139a}{, 139a}\NWlink{nuweb148d}{, 148d}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb10}{10}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb92a}{92a}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}

messages and such.

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap178}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb86c}{} $\langle\,${\it Global variable definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {86c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}

\subsection{Reading a File}

The routine \verb|source_get| returns the next character from the
current source file. It notices newlines and keeps the line counter
\verb|source_line| up to date. It also catches \verb|EOF| and watches
for \verb|@|~characters. All other characters are immediately returned.
We define \verb|source_last| to let us tell which type of scrap we
are defining.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap181}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb87c}{} \verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {87c}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int source_peek;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int source_last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int source_get()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_last = c = source_peek;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EOF:  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle \verb|EOF|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb91b}{91b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '\n': source_line++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle an ``at'' character}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb89}{89}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14a}{14a}\NWlink{nuweb87a}{, 87a}\NWlink{nuweb87b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb87c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb88}{, 88}\NWlink{nuweb92a}{, 92a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb25c}{25c}\NWlink{nuweb26}{, 26}\NWlink{nuweb27a}{, 27a}\NWlink{nuweb27b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb28c}{, 28c}\NWlink{nuweb29a}{, 29a}\NWlink{nuweb30a}{, 30a}\NWlink{nuweb30b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb31a}{, 31a}\NWlink{nuweb32a}{, 32a}\NWlink{nuweb32b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb36}{, 36}\NWlink{nuweb38}{, 38}\NWlink{nuweb39a}{, 39a}\NWlink{nuweb41c}{, 41c}\NWlink{nuweb42a}{, 42a}\NWlink{nuweb43}{, 43}\NWlink{nuweb48a}{, 48a}\NWlink{nuweb48c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb56a}{, 56a}\NWlink{nuweb57c}{, 57c}\NWlink{nuweb57d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb57e}{e}\NWlink{nuweb58a}{, 58a}\NWlink{nuweb62a}{, 62a}\NWlink{nuweb63b}{, 63b}\NWlink{nuweb67b}{, 67b}\NWlink{nuweb70b}{, 70b}\NWlink{nuweb71}{, 71}\NWlink{nuweb73d}{, 73d}\NWlink{nuweb76}{, 76}\NWlink{nuweb77}{, 77}\NWlink{nuweb78c}{, 78c}\NWlink{nuweb79a}{, 79a}\NWlink{nuweb81a}{, 81a}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb90}{, 90}\NWlink{nuweb91b}{, 91b}\NWlink{nuweb97}{, 97}\NWlink{nuweb98}{, 98}\NWlink{nuweb99b}{, 99b}\NWlink{nuweb100}{, 100}\NWlink{nuweb101c}{, 101c}\NWlink{nuweb124}{, 124}\NWlink{nuweb125a}{, 125a}\NWlink{nuweb125b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb126}{, 126}\NWlink{nuweb127a}{, 127a}\NWlink{nuweb127b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb128c}{, 128c}\NWlink{nuweb130}{, 130}\NWlink{nuweb131}{, 131}\NWlink{nuweb132a}{, 132a}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb38}{38}\NWlink{nuweb39a}{, 39a}\NWlink{nuweb54}{, 54}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb30a}{30a}\NWlink{nuweb31a}{, 31a}\NWlink{nuweb32a}{, 32a}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb88}{, 88}\NWlink{nuweb89}{, 89}\NWlink{nuweb90}{, 90}\NWlink{nuweb91b}{, 91b}\NWlink{nuweb92a}{, 92a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\verb|source_ungetc| pushes a read character back to the \verb|source_file|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap182}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb88}{} \verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {88}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void source_ungetc(int *c)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        ungetc(source_peek, source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if(*c == '\n')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_line--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   source_peek=*c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14a}{14a}\NWlink{nuweb87a}{, 87a}\NWlink{nuweb87b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb87c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb88}{, 88}\NWlink{nuweb92a}{, 92a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@source_ungetc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb30b}{30b}\NWlink{nuweb31a}{, 31a}\NWlink{nuweb32b}{, 32b}\NWlink{nuweb63b}{, 63b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
This whole \verb|@|~character handling mess is pretty annoying.
I want to recognize \verb|@i| so I can handle include files correctly.
At the same time, it makes sense to recognize illegal \verb|@|~sequences
and complain; this avoids ever having to check anywhere else.
Unfortunately, I need to avoid tripping over the \verb|@@|~sequence;
hence this whole unsatisfactory \verb|double_at| business.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap183}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb89}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle an ``at'' character}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {89}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (double_at) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    double_at = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'i': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Open an include file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb90}{90}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '#': case 'f': case 'm': case 'u': case 'v':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'd': case 'o': case 'D': case 'O': case 's':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'q': case 'Q': case 'S': case 't':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '*':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\'':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '{': case '}': case '<': case '>': case '|':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '(': case ')': case '[': case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '%': case '_':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ':': case ',': case 'x': case 'c':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '1': case '2': case '3': case '4': case '5':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '6': case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                c = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                double_at = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             fprintf(stderr, "%s: bad %c sequence %c[%d] (%s, line %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                     command_name, nw_char, c, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@double_at@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap184}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb90}{} $\langle\,${\it Open an include file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {90}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char fullname[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  struct incl * p = include_list;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (include_depth >= 10) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: include nesting too deep (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Collect include-file name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb91a}{91a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  stack[include_depth].file = source_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fullname[0] = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (;;) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     strcat(fullname, name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_file = fopen(fullname, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     if (source_file || !p)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     strcpy(fullname, p->name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     strcat(fullname, "/");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!source_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open include file %s\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_file = stack[include_depth].file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     stack[include_depth].name = source_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     stack[include_depth].line = source_line + 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     include_depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_line = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_name = save_string(fullname);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb89}{89}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@incl@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@save_string@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb119a}{119a}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@stack@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87b}{87b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap185}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb91a}{} $\langle\,${\it Collect include-file name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {91a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c != '\n') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected characters after file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb90}{90}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@isgraph@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
If an \verb|EOF| is discovered, the current file must be closed and
input from the next stacked file must be resumed. If no more files are
on the stack, the \verb|EOF| is returned.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap186}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb91b}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle \verb|EOF|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {91b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fclose(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (include_depth) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    include_depth--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_file = stack[include_depth].file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_line = stack[include_depth].line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_name = stack[include_depth].name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87a}{87a}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb86b}{86b}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87c}{87c}, \verb@stack@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb87b}{87b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Opening a File}

The routine \verb|source_open| takes a file name and tries to open the
file. If unsuccessful, it complains and halts. Otherwise, it sets
\verb|source_name|, \verb|source_line|, and \verb|double_at|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap187}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb92a}{} \verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {92a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void source_open(name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_file = fopen(name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!source_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: couldn't open %s\n", command_name, name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  nw_char = '@{\tt @}\verb@';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_name = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_line = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  double_at = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  include_depth = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14a}{14a}\NWlink{nuweb87a}{, 87a}\NWlink{nuweb87b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb87c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb88}{, 88}\NWlink{nuweb92a}{, 92a}.

\mbox{}\verb@     int *page;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    if (first!=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(file, "%d", scrap_array(num).page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else if (scrap_array(num).page != *page)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(file, ", %d", scrap_array(num).page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (scrap_array(num).letter > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputc(scrap_array(num).letter, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (first!=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(", ?", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Warn (only once) about needing to rerun after Latex}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb94c}{94c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (first>=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *page = scrap_array(num).page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\

\NWtarget{nuweb98}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle at-sign during scrap accumulation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {98}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '*':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Collect user-specified index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb100}{100}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}': if (--depth > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              /* else fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push('\0', &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              scrap_ended_with = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              return current_scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle macro invocation in scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb101c}{101c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': case '#': case 'v':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 't':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default :@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@      char new_name[MAX_NAME_LEN];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      char *p = new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      unsigned int sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (c != nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        } while (c != nw_char && !isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        switch (type) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '*':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add user identifier use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb101a}{101a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add user identifier use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb101a}{101a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '|':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add user identifier definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb101b}{101b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    } while (c != nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }while (c == '|' || c == '*' || c == '-' || c == '+');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != '}' && c != ']' && c != ')') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected %c%c in index entry (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb98}{98}.

\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist * p = par;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@   if (a != NULL) {@\\

\mbox{}\verb@      Name* name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Set up name, args and next}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb104b}{104b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (changed){@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Build a new arglist}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb104c}{104c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *ch = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   return a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14b}{14b}\NWlink{nuweb34e}{, 34e}\NWlink{nuweb92b}{, 92b}\NWlink{nuweb92c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb93a}{, 93a}\NWlink{nuweb93c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb94a}{, 94a}\NWlink{nuweb94b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb95c}{, 95c}\NWlink{nuweb95d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb96a}{, 96a}\NWlink{nuweb96b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb102a}{, 102a}\NWlink{nuweb102c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb103a}{, 103a}\NWlink{nuweb103b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb104a}{, 104a}\NWlink{nuweb105a}{, 105a}\NWlink{nuweb106a}{, 106a}\NWlink{nuweb115a}{, 115a}\NWlink{nuweb134b}{, 134b}\NWlink{nuweb134c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135a}{, 135a}\NWlink{nuweb135b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb135c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb136a}{, 136a}\NWlink{nuweb136b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb136c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb138a}{, 138a}\NWlink{nuweb139b}{, 139b}\NWlink{nuweb139c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb144a}{, 144a}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb145a}{, 145a}\NWlink{nuweb146b}{, 146b}\NWlink{nuweb147b}{, 147b}\NWlink{nuweb148a}{, 148a}\NWlink{nuweb148c}{c}.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap218}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb104b}{} $\langle\,${\it Set up name, args and next}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {104b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@next = instance(a->next, par, arg, &changed);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@name = a->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (name == (Name *)1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   Embed_Node * q = (Embed_Node *)arena_getmem(sizeof(Embed_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   q->defs = (Scrap_Node *)a->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   q->args = par;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   args = (Arglist *)q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   changed = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} else if (name != NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  args = instance(a->args, par, arg, &changed);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * p = (char *)a->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (p[0] == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      lookup(p[1] - '1', par, arg, &name, &args);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      changed = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      args = a->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb104a}{104a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@Arglist@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb129b}{129b}, \verb@ARG_CHR@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb127c}{127c}, \verb@Embed_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb132d}{132d}, \verb@instance@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb104a}{104a}, \verb@lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb103b}{103b}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
