\NWtarget{nuweb107}{} $\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|defs->scrap| to \verb|file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {107}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Manager reader;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Parameters local_parameters = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int line_number = scrap_array(defs->scrap).file_line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert debugging information if required}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108b}{108b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reader.scrap = scrap_array(defs->scrap).slab;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reader.index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (delayed_indent)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108c}{108c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (global_indent >= 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           line_number++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           newline = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           delayed_indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108c}{108c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           /* Don't show newlines in embedded fragmants */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           fputs(". . .", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           return;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle tab characters on output}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb109b}{109b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 delayed_indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for macro invocation in scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb109c}{109c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (global_indent >= 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add more indentation \verb@' '@}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108a}{108a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c > ' ') newline = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         delayed_indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb106a}{106a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delayed_indent@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106b}{106b}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Manager@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb95c}{95c}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@Parameters@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb34e}{34e}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb102c}{102c}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@scrap_array@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We need to make sure that we don't overflow \verb|indent_chars[]|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap225}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb108a}{} $\langle\,${\it Add more indentation \hbox{\slshape\sffamily char\/}}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {108a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (global_indent + indent >= MAX_INDENT) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           "Error! maximum indentation exceeded in \"%s\".\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  indent_chars[global_indent + indent] = @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily char\/}\verb@;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb107}{107}\NWlink{nuweb109b}{, 109b}\NWlink{nuweb109c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@MAX_INDENT@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb83b}{83b}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap226}\raggedright\small

\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (debug_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(file, "\n#line %d \"%s\"\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          line_number, scrap_array(defs->scrap).file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108c}{108c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap228}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb108d}{} $\langle\,${\it Put out the indent}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {108d}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (tab_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for (indent=0; indent<global_indent; indent++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for (indent=0; indent<global_indent; indent++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(indent_chars[indent], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb35}{35}\NWlink{nuweb108c}{, 108c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Indent will be suppressed if the next character is a newline or
if the next two characters are \verb|@#|. If the next two characters
are \verb|@<|, we suppress the indent for now but mark that it
may be needed when the next fragment is started.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap229}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb109a}{} $\langle\,${\it Indent suppressed}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {109a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@c1 == '\n'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@|| c1 == nw_char && (c2 == '#' || (delayed_indent |= (c2 == '<')))@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb108c}{108c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delayed_indent@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106b}{106b}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap230}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb109b}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle tab characters on output}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {109b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (tab_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb55c}{55c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('\t', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (global_indent >= 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add more indentation \verb@'\t'@}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108a}{108a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\NWtarget{nuweb109c}{} $\langle\,${\it Check for macro invocation in scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {109c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 't': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy fragment title into file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb112c}{112c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'c': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy block comment from scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb33b}{33b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy file name into file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb110c}{110c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy label from scrap into file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb110a}{110a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'v': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy version info into file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb57a}{57a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy macro into \verb|file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb111}{111}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert debugging information if required}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108b}{108b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle macro parameter substitution}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb35}{35}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if(c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              if (global_indent >= 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add more indentation \verb@' '@}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb108a}{108a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          /* ignore, since we should already have a warning */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\NWtarget{nuweb111}{} $\langle\,${\it Copy macro into \verb|file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {111}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *a = pop_scrap_name(&reader, &local_parameters);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = a->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int changed;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist * args = instance(a->args, inArgs, inParams, &changed);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int i, narg;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * * inParams = name->arg;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *q = args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->mark) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: recursive macro discovered involving <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs && !defs->quoted) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps comment this macro}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb112a}{112a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name->mark = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    indent = write_scraps(file, spelling, name->defs, global_indent + indent,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                          indent_chars, debug_flag, tab_flag, indent_flag,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                          comment_flag, args, name->arg,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                          local_parameters, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    indent -= global_indent;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name->mark = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (delayed_indent)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      for (i = indent + global_indent; --i >= 0; )@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(file, "%c<",  nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->sector == 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputc('+', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Comment this macro use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb113a}{113a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(file, "%c>",  nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!defs->quoted && !tex_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "%s: macro never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb109c}{109c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Arglist@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb129b}{129b}, \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17d}{17d}, \verb@delayed_indent@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106b}{106b}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@instance@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb104a}{104a}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@pop_scrap_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb105a}{105a}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@tex_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb16}{16}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@write_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb106a}{106a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}

\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap236}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb112a}{} $\langle\,${\it Perhaps comment this macro}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {112a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (comment_flag && newline) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps put a delayed indent}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb112b}{112b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(comment_begin[comment_flag], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Comment this macro use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb113a}{113a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (xref_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(file, name->defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (comment_end)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(comment_end[comment_flag], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   putc('\n', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (!delayed_indent)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      for (i = indent + global_indent; --i >= 0; )@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\NWtarget{nuweb113a}{} $\langle\,${\it Comment this macro use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {113a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@narg = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@while (*p != '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (*p == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (q == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       if (defs->quoted)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fprintf(file, "%c'%s%c'", nw_char, inParams[narg], nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fprintf(file, "'%s'", inParams[narg]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      comment_ArglistElement(file, q, defs->quoted);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      q = q->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    narg++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(*p++, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\NWtarget{nuweb113b}{} $\langle\,${\it Forward declarations for scraps.c}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {113b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void@\\
\mbox{}\verb@comment_ArglistElement(FILE * file, Arglist * args, int quote)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = args->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist *q = args->args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (quote)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fprintf(file, "%c'%s%c'", nw_char, (char *)q, nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fprintf(file, "'%s'", (char *)q);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else if (name == (Name *)1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Include an embedded scrap in comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb113c}{113c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Include a fragment use in comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb114a}{114a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@comment_ArglistElement@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb113a}{113a}\NWlink{nuweb114a}{, 114a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Arglist@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb129b}{129b}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap242}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb114a}{} $\langle\,${\it Include a fragment use in comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {114a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@char * p = name->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (quote)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputc(nw_char, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputc('<', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (quote && name->sector == 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputc('+', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@while (*p != '\000') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (*p == ARG_CHR) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    comment_ArglistElement(file, q, quote);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q = q->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(*p++, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (quote)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputc(nw_char, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputc('>', file);@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb113b}{113b}.

\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small

\NWtarget{nuweb115a}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {115a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void collect_numbers(aux_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *aux_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (number_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for (i=1; i<scraps; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      scrap_array(i).page = i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    FILE *aux_file = fopen(aux_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    already_warned = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (aux_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      char aux_line[500];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (fgets(aux_line, 500, aux_file)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int scrap_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int page_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        char dummy[50];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (3 == sscanf(aux_line, "\\newlabel{scrap%d}{%[^}]}{%d}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                        &scrap_number, dummy, &page_number)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (scrap_number < scraps)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            scrap_array(scrap_number).page = page_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Warn (only once) about needing to rerun after Latex}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb94c}{94c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fclose(aux_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add letters to scraps with duplicate page numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb115b}{115b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap254}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb118b}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {118b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@enum { LESS, GREATER, EQUAL, PREFIX, EXTENSION };@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static int compare(x, y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int len, result;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int xl = strlen(x);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int yl = strlen(y);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int xp = x[xl - 1] == ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int yp = y[yl - 1] == ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (xp) xl--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (yp) yl--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  len = xl < yl ? xl : yl;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  result = strncmp(x, y, len);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (result < 0) return GREATER;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (result > 0) return LESS;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (xl < yl) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (xp) return EXTENSION;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else return LESS;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (xl > yl) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (yp) return PREFIX;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else return GREATER;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else return EQUAL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14c}{14c}\NWlink{nuweb118b}{, 118b}\NWlink{nuweb119a}{, 119a}\NWlink{nuweb119b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb120b}{, 120b}\NWlink{nuweb121a}{, 121a}\NWlink{nuweb122}{, 122}\NWlink{nuweb124}{, 124}\NWlink{nuweb126}{, 126}\NWlink{nuweb129a}{, 129a}\NWlink{nuweb129c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb130}{, 130}\NWlink{nuweb133c}{, 133c}\NWlink{nuweb134a}{, 134a}.

\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static char * found_name = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Name *prefix_add(rt, spelling, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name **rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  int cmp;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    case GREATER:   rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case LESS:      rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@                    found_name = node->spelling;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@                       rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@                       rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    if (cmp == EXTENSION)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       node->spelling = save_string(spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case PREFIX:    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for ambiguous prefix}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb120a}{120a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    node = *rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Create new name entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb123}{123}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\

Since a very short prefix might match more than one fragment name, I need
to check for other matches to avoid mistakes. Basically, I simply
continue the search down {\em both\/} branches of the tree.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap257}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb120a}{} $\langle\,${\it Check for ambiguous prefix}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {120a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (ambiguous_prefix(node->llink, spelling, sector) ||@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      ambiguous_prefix(node->rlink, spelling, sector))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            "%s: ambiguous prefix %c<%s...%c> (%s, line %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, spelling, nw_char, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

Rob Shillingsburg suggested that I organize the index of
user-specified identifiers more traditionally; that is, not relying on
strict {\small ASCII} comparisons via \verb|strcmp|. Ideally, we'd like
to see the index ordered like this:
\begin{quote}
\begin{flushleft}
aardvark \\
Adam \\
atom \\
Atomic \\
atoms
\end{flushleft}
\end{quote}
The function \verb|robs_strcmp| implements the desired predicate.
It returns -2 for alphabetically less-than, -1 for less-than but only
differing in case, zero for equal, 1 for greater-than but only in case
and 2 for alphabetically greater-than.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap259}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb121a}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {121a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int robs_strcmp(x, y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int cmp = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   for (; *x && *y; x++, y++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip invisibles on \verb@x@}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb121b}{121b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip invisibles on \verb@y@}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb121b}{121b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (*x == *y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         continue;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (islower(*x) && toupper(*x) == *y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (!cmp) cmp = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         continue;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (islower(*y) && *x == toupper(*y))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (!cmp) cmp = -1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         continue;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return 2*(toupper(*x) - toupper(*y));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (*x)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (*y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   return cmp;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14c}{14c}\NWlink{nuweb118b}{, 118b}\NWlink{nuweb119a}{, 119a}\NWlink{nuweb119b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb120b}{, 120b}\NWlink{nuweb121a}{, 121a}\NWlink{nuweb122}{, 122}\NWlink{nuweb124}{, 124}\NWlink{nuweb126}{, 126}\NWlink{nuweb129a}{, 129a}\NWlink{nuweb129c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb130}{, 130}\NWlink{nuweb133c}{, 133c}\NWlink{nuweb134a}{, 134a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@robs_strcmp@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb64c}{64c}\NWlink{nuweb122}{, 122}\NWlink{nuweb123}{, 123}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{, 144b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@islower@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@toupper@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Certain character sequences are invisible when printed. We don't want
them to be considered for the alphabetical ordering.

\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *node = *rt;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    int result = robs_strcmp(node->spelling, spelling);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    else if (result < 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       found_name = node->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       if (node->sector > sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       else if (node->sector < sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Create new name entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb123}{123}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  node->arg[4] =@\\

Name terminated by whitespace.  Also check for ``per-file'' flags. Keep
skipping white space until we reach scrap.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap263}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb124}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {124}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *collect_file_name()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[MAX_NAME_LEN];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int start_line = source_line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get(), c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p == name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* File names are always global. */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  new_name = name_add(&file_names, name, 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle optional per-file flags}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb125a}{125a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c2 = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != nw_char || (c2 != '{' && c2 != '(' && c2 != '[')) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected %c{, %c[, or %c( after file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, nw_char, nw_char, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\NWtarget{nuweb125a}{} $\langle\,${\it Handle optional per-file flags}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {125a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == '-') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 't': new_name->tab_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 'd': new_name->debug_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 'i': new_name->indent_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 'c': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Get comment delimiters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb125b}{125b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          default : fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected per-file flag (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      } while (!isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb124}{124}.

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\mbox{}\verb@   new_name->comment_flag = 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else if (c == 'p')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   new_name->comment_flag = 3;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fprintf(stderr, "%s: Unrecognised comment flag (%s, %d)\n",@\\

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap267}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb126}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {126}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *collect_macro_name()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[MAX_NAME_LEN];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char args[1000];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * arg[9];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char * argp = args;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int argc = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int start_line = source_line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get(), c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '+') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Name * node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ' ':  *p++ = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip until scrap begins, then return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb128c}{128c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for terminating at-sequence and return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb127a}{127a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected fragment name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return NULL;  /* unreachable return to avoid warnings on some compilers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\NWtarget{nuweb127a}{} $\langle\,${\it Check for terminating at-sequence and return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {127a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb128b}{128b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             return install_args(node, argc, arg);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '\'': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Enter the next argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb127b}{127b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      "%s: unexpected %c%c in fragment definition name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (i = 0; i < argc; i++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->arg[i] == NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      name->arg[i] = save_string(arg[i]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small

\NWtarget{nuweb130}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {130}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Arglist * collect_scrap_name(int current_scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[MAX_NAME_LEN];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist * head = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Arglist ** tail = &head;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '+')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c == ' ' || c == '\t')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ' ':  *p++ = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Look for end of scrap name and return}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb131}{131}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (!isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           "%s: unexpected character in fragment name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected end of file (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return NULL;  /* unreachable return to avoid warnings on some compilers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}

\NWtarget{nuweb131}{} $\langle\,${\it Look for end of scrap name and return}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {131}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name * node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '\'': {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add plain string argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb132a}{132a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p++ = ARG_CHR;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9': {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add a propagated argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb132b}{132b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p++ = ARG_CHR;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add an inline scrap argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb132c}{132c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p++ = ARG_CHR;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add macro call argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb133a}{133a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p++ = ARG_CHR;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        scrap_name_has_parameters = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb128b}{128b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        return buildArglist(node, head);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '>':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        scrap_name_has_parameters = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb128b}{128b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        return buildArglist(node, head);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      "%s: unexpected %c%c in fragment invocation name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb130}{130}.

A plain string argument has no name and a string as a value.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap280}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb132a}{} $\langle\,${\it Add plain string argument}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {132a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@char buff[MAX_NAME_LEN];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@char * s = buff;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int c, c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@while ((c = source_get()) != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c==nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c2 = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c2=='\'')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *s++ = c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *s++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@*s = '\000';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add buff to current arg list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb133b}{133b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

and and a string of \verb|ARG_CHAR| followed by a digit as value.

\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14c}{14c}\NWlink{nuweb118b}{, 118b}\NWlink{nuweb119a}{, 119a}\NWlink{nuweb119b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb120b}{, 120b}\NWlink{nuweb121a}{, 121a}\NWlink{nuweb122}{, 122}\NWlink{nuweb124}{, 124}\NWlink{nuweb126}{, 126}\NWlink{nuweb129a}{, 129a}\NWlink{nuweb129c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb130}{, 130}\NWlink{nuweb133c}{, 133c}\NWlink{nuweb134a}{, 134a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@reverse_lists@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb34d}{34d}\NWlink{nuweb118a}{, 118a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@reverse@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134a}{134a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
Just for fun, here's a non-recursive version of the traditional list
reversal code. Note that it reverses the list in place; that is, it
does no new allocations.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap287}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb134a}{} \verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {134a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static Scrap_Node *reverse(a)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Scrap_Node *a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (a) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *b = a->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    a->next = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (b) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Scrap_Node *c = b->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      b->next = a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      a = b;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      b = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14c}{14c}\NWlink{nuweb118b}{, 118b}\NWlink{nuweb119a}{, 119a}\NWlink{nuweb119b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb120b}{, 120b}\NWlink{nuweb121a}{, 121a}\NWlink{nuweb122}{, 122}\NWlink{nuweb124}{, 124}\NWlink{nuweb126}{, 126}\NWlink{nuweb129a}{, 129a}\NWlink{nuweb129c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb130}{, 130}\NWlink{nuweb133c}{, 133c}\NWlink{nuweb134a}{, 134a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@reverse@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb133c}{133c}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\section{Searching for Index Entries} \label{search}

Given the array of scraps and a set of index entries, we need to
search all the scraps for occurrences of each entry. The obvious
approach to this problem would be quite expensive for large documents;
however, there is an interesting  paper describing an efficient
solution~\cite{aho:75}.


\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap288}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb134b}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {134b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@typedef struct name_node {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  struct name_node *next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} Name_Node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\NWtarget{nuweb135c}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {135c}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static Goto_Node *goto_lookup(c, g)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Goto_Node *g;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Move_Node *m = g->moves;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (m && m->c != c)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    m = m->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (m)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return m->state;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap297}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb137a}{} $\langle\,${\it Perhaps |return| a character from the current arg}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {137a}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (a->pv != NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char c = *a->pv++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (c != '\0')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   a->pv = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   return ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb136c}{136c}.

\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
I'm pretty sure that only the first case is ever used. I don't think
the others can occur in this context, which makes the whole
|ArgManager| thing doubtful.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap306}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb140}{} $\langle\,${\it Extend goto graph with \verb|tree->spelling|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {140}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int depth = 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = tree->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c = *p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Goto_Node *q = root[c];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name_Node * last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!q) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q = (Goto_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Goto_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    root[c] = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->fail = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->output = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->next = depths[1];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    depths[1] = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c = *p++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *new = goto_lookup(c, q);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!new) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Move_Node *new_move = (Move_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Move_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new = (Goto_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Goto_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->fail = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->output = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->state = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->c = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->next = q->moves;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      q->moves = new_move;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (depth == max_depth) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node **new_depths =@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            (Goto_Node **) arena_getmem(2*depth*sizeof(Goto_Node *));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        max_depth = 2 * depth;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        for (i=0; i<depth; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          new_depths[i] = depths[i];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        depths = new_depths;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        for (i=depth; i<max_depth; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          depths[i] = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->next = depths[depth];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      depths[depth] = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  last = q->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output = (Name_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Name_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output->next = last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output->name = tree;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb139c}{139c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@depths@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135c}{135c}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134c}{134c}, \verb@max_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}, \verb@Move_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135a}{135a}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134b}{134b}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap307}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb141}{} $\langle\,${\it Build failure functions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {141}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int depth;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (depth=1; depth<max_depth; depth++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *r = depths[depth];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (r) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Move_Node *m = r->moves;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (m) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        char a = m->c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node *s = m->state;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node *state = r->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        while (state && !goto_lookup(a, state))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          state = state->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (state)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          s->fail = goto_lookup(a, state);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          s->fail = root[a];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (s->fail) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Name_Node *p = s->fail->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          while (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            Name_Node *q = (Name_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Name_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            q->name = p->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            q->next = s->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            s->output = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        m = m->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      r = r->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb139b}{139b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@depths@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135c}{135c}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134c}{134c}, \verb@max_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}, \verb@Move_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135a}{135a}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134b}{134b}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\subsection{Searching the Scraps}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap308}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb142}{} $\langle\,${\it Search scraps}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {142}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (i=1; i<scraps; i++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char c, last = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Manager rd;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    ArgManager reader;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *state = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    rd.prev = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    rd.scrap = scrap_array(i).slab;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    rd.index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    reader.m = &rd;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    reader.a = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = argpop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (state && !goto_lookup(c, state))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = state->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (state)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = goto_lookup(c, state);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = root[c];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over at at}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb143a}{143a}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over a scrap use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb143b}{143b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over a block comment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb34b}{34b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      last = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = argpop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (state && state->output) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Name_Node *p = state->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Name *name = p->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (!reject_match(name, c, &reader) &&@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              scrap_array(i).sector == name->sector &&@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              (!name->uses || name->uses->scrap != i)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            Scrap_Node *new_use =@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                (Scrap_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Scrap_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            new_use->scrap = i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            new_use->next = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            name->uses = new_use;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            if (!scrap_is_in(name->defs, i))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              add_uses(&(scrap_array(i).uses), name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        } while (p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb139b}{139b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@add_uses@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb144b}{144b}, \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}, \verb@ArgManager@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb136a}{136a}, \verb@argpop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb136c}{136c}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135c}{135c}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134c}{134c}, \verb@Manager@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb95c}{95c}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb134b}{134b}, \verb@reject_match@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb148a}{148a}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb135b}{135b}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@scrap_array@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@scrap_is_in@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb144a}{144a}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb116d}{116d}.

\mbox{}\verb@      Uses *new = arena_getmem(sizeof(Uses));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->next = p;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->defn = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *q = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\

\subsubsection{Rejecting Matches}

A problem with simple substring matching is that the string ``he''
would match longer strings like ``she'' and ``her.'' Norman Ramsey
suggested examining the characters occurring immediately before and
after a match and rejecting the match if it appears to be part of a
longer token. Of course, the concept of {\sl token\/} is
language-dependent, so we may be occasionally mistaken.
For the present, we'll consider the mechanism an experiment.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap322}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb147b}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {147b}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@#define sym_char(c) (isalnum(c) || (c) == '_')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static int op_char(c)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '!':           case '#': case '%': case '$': case '^':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '&': case '*': case '-': case '+': case '=': case '/':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': case '~': case '<': case '>':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return c==nw_char ? TRUE : FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14b}{14b}\NWlink{nuweb34e}{, 34e}\NWlink{nuweb92b}{, 92b}\NWlink{nuweb92c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb93a}{, 93a}\NWlink{nuweb93c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb94a}{, 94a}\NWlink{nuweb94b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb95c}{, 95c}\NWlink{nuweb95d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb96a}{, 96a}\NWlink{nuweb96b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb102a}{, 102a}\NWlink{nuweb102c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb103a}{, 103a}\NWlink{nuweb103b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb104a}{, 104a}\NWlink{nuweb105a}{, 105a}\NWlink{nuweb106a}{, 106a}\NWlink{nuweb115a}{, 115a}\NWlink{nuweb134b}{, 134b}\NWlink{nuweb134c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135a}{, 135a}\NWlink{nuweb135b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb135c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb136a}{, 136a}\NWlink{nuweb136b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb136c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb138a}{, 138a}\NWlink{nuweb139b}{, 139b}\NWlink{nuweb139c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb144a}{, 144a}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb145a}{, 145a}\NWlink{nuweb146b}{, 146b}\NWlink{nuweb147b}{, 147b}\NWlink{nuweb148a}{, 148a}\NWlink{nuweb148c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@op_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb148a}{148a}, \verb@sym_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb148a}{148a}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb17b}{17b}\NWlink{nuweb17c}{c}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap323}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb148a}{} \verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {148a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static int reject_match(name, post, reader)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char post;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     ArgManager *reader;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int len = strlen(name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char first = name->spelling[0];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char last = name->spelling[len - 1];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char prev = prev_char(reader, len);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (sym_char(last) && sym_char(post)) return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (sym_char(first) && sym_char(prev)) return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (op_char(last) && op_char(post)) return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (op_char(first) && op_char(prev)) return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return FALSE; /* Here is 148a-01 */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14b}{14b}\NWlink{nuweb34e}{, 34e}\NWlink{nuweb92b}{, 92b}\NWlink{nuweb92c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb93a}{, 93a}\NWlink{nuweb93c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb94a}{, 94a}\NWlink{nuweb94b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb95c}{, 95c}\NWlink{nuweb95d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb96a}{, 96a}\NWlink{nuweb96b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb102a}{, 102a}\NWlink{nuweb102c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb103a}{, 103a}\NWlink{nuweb103b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb104a}{, 104a}\NWlink{nuweb105a}{, 105a}\NWlink{nuweb106a}{, 106a}\NWlink{nuweb115a}{, 115a}\NWlink{nuweb134b}{, 134b}\NWlink{nuweb134c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135a}{, 135a}\NWlink{nuweb135b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb135c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb135d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb136a}{, 136a}\NWlink{nuweb136b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb136c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb138a}{, 138a}\NWlink{nuweb139b}{, 139b}\NWlink{nuweb139c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb144a}{, 144a}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb145a}{, 145a}\NWlink{nuweb146b}{, 146b}\NWlink{nuweb147b}{, 147b}\NWlink{nuweb148a}{, 148a}\NWlink{nuweb148c}{c}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@reject_match@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb139b}{139b}\NWlink{nuweb142}{, 142}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@ArgManager@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb136a}{136a}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}, \verb@first@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb117a}{117a}, \verb@op_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb147b}{147b}, \verb@prev_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb138a}{138a}, \verb@strlen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@sym_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb147b}{147b}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb12a}{12a}.

\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}

\mbox{}\verb@         {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily Found\/}\verb@@\\

\mbox{}\verb@         }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          @\hbox{\slshape\sffamily Notfound\/}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\section{Memory Management} \label{memory-management}

I manage memory using a simple scheme inspired by Hanson's idea of
{\em arenas\/}~\cite{hanson:90}.
Basically, I allocate all the storage required when processing a
source file (primarily for names and scraps) using calls to
\verb|arena_getmem(n)|, where \verb|n| specifies the number of bytes to
be allocated. When the storage is no longer required, the entire arena
is freed with a single call to  \verb|arena_free()|. Both operations
are quite fast.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap337}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb151b}{} $\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {151b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void *arena_getmem();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@extern void arena_free();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb25a}{25a}\NWlink{nuweb39b}{, 39b}\NWlink{nuweb52b}{, 52b}\NWlink{nuweb55b}{, 55b}\NWlink{nuweb69a}{, 69a}\NWlink{nuweb82b}{, 82b}\NWlink{nuweb86a}{, 86a}\NWlink{nuweb93b}{, 93b}\NWlink{nuweb102b}{, 102b}\NWlink{nuweb114b}{, 114b}\NWlink{nuweb118a}{, 118a}\NWlink{nuweb128d}{, 128d}\NWlink{nuweb139a}{, 139a}\NWlink{nuweb148d}{, 148d}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb10}{10}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_free@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb153}{153}, \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap338}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb151c}{} \verb@"arena.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {151c}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@typedef struct chunk {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  struct chunk *next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *limit;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *avail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} Chunk;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14d}{14d}\NWlink{nuweb151c}{, 151c}\NWlink{nuweb151d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb152a}{, 152a}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@Chunk@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}\NWlink{nuweb152b}{, 152b}\NWlink{nuweb152c}{c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
We define an empty chunk called \verb|first|. The variable \verb|arena| points
at the current chunk of memory; it's initially pointed at \verb|first|.
As soon as some storage is required, a ``real'' chunk of memory will
be allocated and attached to \verb|first->next|; storage will be
allocated from the new chunk (and later chunks if necessary).
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap339}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb151d}{} \verb@"arena.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {151d}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static Chunk first = { NULL, NULL, NULL };@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static Chunk *arena = &first;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14d}{14d}\NWlink{nuweb151c}{, 151c}\NWlink{nuweb151d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb152a}{, 152a}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@arena@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}\NWlink{nuweb152b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb152c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}, \verb@first@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb94a}{94a}\NWlink{nuweb145c}{, 145c}\NWlink{nuweb146a}{, 146a}\NWlink{nuweb147a}{, 147a}\NWlink{nuweb148a}{, 148a}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}\NWlink{nuweb154}{, 154}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Chunk@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151c}{151c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Allocating Memory}

The routine \verb|arena_getmem(n)| returns a pointer to (at least)
\verb|n| bytes of memory. Note that \verb|n| is rounded up to ensure
that returned pointers are always aligned.  We align to the nearest
8-byte segment, since that'll satisfy the more common 2-byte and
4-byte alignment restrictions too.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap340}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb152a}{} \verb@"arena.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {152a}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void *arena_getmem(n)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     size_t n;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = arena->avail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  n = (n + 7) & ~7;             /* ensuring alignment to 8 bytes */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q = p + n;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (q <= arena->limit) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    arena->avail = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return p;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Find a new chunk of memory}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb152b}{152b}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14d}{14d}\NWlink{nuweb151c}{, 151c}\NWlink{nuweb151d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb152a}{, 152a}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb20b}{20b}\NWlink{nuweb24a}{, 24a}\NWlink{nuweb28b}{, 28b}\NWlink{nuweb37}{, 37}\NWlink{nuweb93c}{, 93c}\NWlink{nuweb95d}{, 95d}\NWlink{nuweb96c}{, 96c}\NWlink{nuweb101a}{, 101a}\NWlink{nuweb101b}{b}\NWlink{nuweb102a}{, 102a}\NWlink{nuweb104b}{, 104b}\NWlink{nuweb104c}{c}\NWlink{nuweb119a}{, 119a}\NWlink{nuweb123}{, 123}\NWlink{nuweb129c}{, 129c}\NWlink{nuweb132c}{, 132c}\NWlink{nuweb139b}{, 139b}\NWlink{nuweb140}{, 140}\NWlink{nuweb141}{, 141}\NWlink{nuweb142}{, 142}\NWlink{nuweb144b}{, 144b}\NWlink{nuweb149d}{, 149d}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@size_t@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
If the current chunk doesn't have adequate space (at least \verb|n|
bytes) we examine the rest of the list of chunks (starting at
\verb|arena->next|) looking for a chunk with adequate space. If \verb|n|
is very large, we may not find it right away or we may not find a
suitable chunk at all.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap341}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb152b}{} $\langle\,${\it Find a new chunk of memory}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {152b}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Chunk *ap = arena;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Chunk *np = ap->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (np) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char *v = sizeof(Chunk) + (char *) np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (v + n <= np->limit) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      np->avail = v + n;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      arena = np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return v;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    ap = np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    np = ap->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Allocate a new chunk of memory}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb152c}{152c}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb152a}{152a}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@Chunk@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151c}{151c}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
If there isn't a suitable chunk of memory on the free list, then we
need to allocate a new one.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap342}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb152c}{} $\langle\,${\it Allocate a new chunk of memory}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {152c}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  size_t m = n + 10000;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  np = (Chunk *) malloc(m);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  np->limit = m + (char *) np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  np->avail = n + sizeof(Chunk) + (char *) np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  np->next = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  ap->next = np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  arena = np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return sizeof(Chunk) + (char *) np;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb152b}{152b}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@Chunk@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151c}{151c}, \verb@malloc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@size_t@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Freeing Memory}

To free all the memory in the arena, we need only point \verb|arena|
back to the first empty chunk.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth}\label{scrap343}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb153}{} \verb@"arena.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {153}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void arena_free()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  arena = &first;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}
\footnotesize
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb14d}{14d}\NWlink{nuweb151c}{, 151c}\NWlink{nuweb151d}{d}\NWlink{nuweb152a}{, 152a}\NWlink{nuweb153}{, 153}.
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_free@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb24b}{24b}\NWlink{nuweb151b}{, 151b}.\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@first@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}.
\item{}
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\vspace{4ex}
\end{flushleft}
\chapter{Man page}

Here is the UNIX man page for nuweb:

\begin{flushleft} \small\label{scrap344}\raggedright\small
\NWtarget{nuweb154}{} \verb@"nuweb.1"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize {154}}$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@.TH NUWEB 1 "local 3/22/95"@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH NAME@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Nuweb, a literate programming tool@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH SYNOPSIS@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.B nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fBnuweb\fP [options] [file] ...@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH DESCRIPTION@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I Nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@is a literate programming tool like Knuth's@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I WEB,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@only simpler.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@A@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@file contains program source code interleaved with documentation.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@When@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@is given a@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@file, it writes the program file(s),@\\
\mbox{}\verb@and also@\\
\mbox{}\verb@produces,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I LaTeX@\\
\mbox{}\verb@source for typeset documentation.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH COMMAND LINE OPTIONS@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-t\fP Suppresses generation of the {\tt .tex} file.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-o\fP Suppresses generation of the output files.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-d\fP List dangling identifier references in indexes.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-c\fP Forces output files to overwrite old files of the same@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  name without comparing for equality first.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-v\fP The verbose flag. Forces output of progress reports.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-n\fP Forces sequential numbering of scraps (instead of page@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  numbers).@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-s\fP Doesn't print list of scraps making up file at end of@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  each scrap.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-p path\fP Prepend path to the filenames for all the output files.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-V string\fP Provide the string for replacement of the @{\tt @}\verb@v@\\
\mbox{}\verb@operation. This is intended as a means for including version@\\
\mbox{}\verb@information in generated output.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-x\fP Include cross-references in comments in output files.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-h options\fP Turn on hyperlinks using the hyperref package of@\\
\mbox{}\verb@LaTeX and provide the options to the package.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-r\fP Turn on hyperlinks using the hyperref package of@\\
\mbox{}\verb@LaTeX, with the package options being in the text.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-I path\fP Provide a directory to search for included files. This@\\
\mbox{}\verb@may appear several times.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH FORMAT OF NUWEB FILES@\\
\mbox{}\verb@A@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@file contains mostly ordinary@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I LaTeX.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@The file is read and copied to output (.tex file) unless a@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@command is encountered. All@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@commands start with an ``at-sign'' (@{\tt @}\verb@).@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Files and fragments are defined with the following commands:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@o \fIfile-name flags  scrap\fP  where scrap is smaller than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@O \fIfile-name flags  scrap\fP  where scrap is bigger than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@d \fIfragment-name scrap\fP. Where scrap is smallar than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@D \fIfragment-name scrap\fP. Where scrap is bigger than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@q \fIfragment-name scrap\fP. Where scrap is smallar than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@The scrap is not expanded in the output, allowing you to construct@\\
\mbox{}\verb@output files which can, perhaps after further processing, be input to@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@Q \fIfragment-name scrap\fP. Where scrap is bigger than one page.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Likewise.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Scraps have specific begin and end@\\
\mbox{}\verb@markers;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@which begin and end marker you use determines how the scrap will be@\\
\mbox{}\verb@typeset in the .tex file:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB@{\tt @}\verb@{\fP...\fB@{\tt @}\verb@}\fP for verbatim "terminal style" formatting or,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@with the -l flag, LaTeX listing package.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB@{\tt @}\verb@[\fP...\fB@{\tt @}\verb@]\fP for LaTeX paragraph mode formatting, and@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB@{\tt @}\verb@(\fP...\fB@{\tt @}\verb@)\fP for LaTeX math mode formmating.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Any amount of whitespace@\\
\mbox{}\verb@(including carriage returns) may appear between a name and the@\\
\mbox{}\verb@begining of a scrap.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Several code/file scraps may have the same name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@concatenates their definitions to produce a single scrap.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Code scrap definitions are like macro definitions;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@extracts a program by expanding one scrap.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@The definition of that scrap contains references to other scraps, which are@\\
\mbox{}\verb@themselves expanded, and so on.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fINuweb\fP's output is readable; it preserves the indentation of expanded@\\
\mbox{}\verb@scraps with respect to the scraps in which they appear.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH PER FILE OPTIONS@\\
\mbox{}\verb@When defining an output file, the programmer has the option of using flags@\\
\mbox{}\verb@to control the output.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-d\fR option,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I Nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@will emit line number indications at scrap boundaries.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-i\fR option,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.I Nuweb@\\
\mbox{}\verb@supresses the indentation of fragments (useful for \fBFortran\fR).@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-t\fP option makes \fInuweb\fP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@copy tabs untouched from input to output.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fB-c\fIx\fP Include comments in the output file.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fIx\fP may be \fBc\fP for C-style comments, \fB+\fP for C++ and@\\
\mbox{}\verb@\fBp\fP for perl and similar.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH MINOR COMMANDS@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@    Causes a single ``at-sign'' to be copied into the output.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@\_    Causes the text between it and the next {\tt @{\tt @}\verb@\_} to be made bold@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        (for keywords, etc.) in the formatted document@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@%     Comments out a line so that it doesn't appear in the output.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@i     \fBfilename\fR causes the file named to be included.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@f     Creates an index of output files.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@m     Creates an index of fragments.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\tt @}\verb@u     Creates an index of user-specified identifiers.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@To mark an identifier for inclusion in the index, it must be mentioned@\\
\mbox{}\verb@at the end of the scrap it was defined in. The line starts@\\
\mbox{}\verb@with @{\tt @}\verb@| and ends with the \fBend of scrap\fP mark \fB@{\tt @}\verb@}\fP.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH ERROR MESSAGES@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH BUGS@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.PP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH AUTHOR@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Preston Briggs.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Internet address \fBpreston@{\tt @}\verb@cs.rice.edu\fP.@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.SH MAINTAINER@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Simon Wright@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Internet address \fBsimon@{\tt @}\verb@pushface.org\fP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@.br@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Keith Harwood@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Internet address \fBKeith.Harwood@{\tt @}\verb@vitalmis.com\fP@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1.5ex}

\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb11}{11}, \verb@first@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb151d}{151d}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb93a}{93a}, \verb@search@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb139b}{139b}.

\end{flushleft}
\chapter{Indices} \label{indices}

Three sets of indices can be created automatically: an index of file
names, an index of fragment names, and an index of user-specified
identifiers. An index entry includes the name of the entry, where it
was defined, and where it was referenced.

\section{Identifiers}

Knuth prints his index of identifiers in a two-column format.
I could force this automatically by emitting the \verb|\twocolumn|
command; but this has the side effect of forcing a new page.
Therefore, it seems better to leave it this up to the user.
